# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
This is present as there are enough
slits in the grating for most waves
to have a destructive interference. ^kCBza4NB

This is a small 'd' as it is reserved for
diffraction gratings, unlike the large 'D'
in double and single slit patterns. ^dZFBIISE

Take care not to slip here with
proper calculation. The grating
(in this case) is 300 lines per mm.
It will be stated in the exam. ^y2HdT96F
